  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383846535i/6683671.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I love him, I need him, his Mine.... The word mine was probably used over <b>
  <u>200 times</u>
</b>, I kid you not,<br><br><br>Turn the page..<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383846535ra/6683672.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Repeat<br>Turn the page...<br>Repeat</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383846535i/6683673.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>Next topic:</u><br><br><b>Oh I want him so bad<br>Oh I need him so bad<br>On I'm so wet....</b><br><br><i>She was so wet all the time I was starting to wonder if she had a tube of lubbe attached to her Vijayjay!!!!!!</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383846535ra/6683674.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I honestly feel the author used soooo many of the same lines to fill pages.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383846535i/6683675._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So all in all this book is a huge let down.<br>Good luck to all who invests time reading it. Hope you like it better than I did!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383846535ra/6683676.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_686235370" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/686235370" />
    <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei"><img alt="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1421992465p2/2551178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/686235370?book_show_action=true">Aug 04, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei">Lady Vigilante (Feifei)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=douchenugget">douchenugget</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=netgalley-edelweiss">netgalley-edelweiss</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=read-to-review">read-to-review</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer686235370" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5765401080147107914"><b> 2.5 Dull Stars</b><br/><br/>Note: If you are a hard-core Remy fan and you INFINITE-STARRED Real, don’t bother reading this review. You’re wasting your time. Just go get a copy of Mine because chances are you’ll love it too.<br/><br/>EDIT: Forgot to add this, but Mine is NOT in Remy's POV. All in Brooke's.....<br/><br/>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br/><br/>I’m going to be ranting so apologies ahead of time. <br/><br/><b>
  <u>If you like books with exaggerated intensity, this is the one for you.</u>
</b><br/><br/>This writing is...<i>interesting.</i> *cocks head*</span>
  <span id="freeText5765401080147107914" style="display:none"><b> 2.5 Dull Stars</b><br /><br />Note: If you are a hard-core Remy fan and you INFINITE-STARRED Real, don’t bother reading this review. You’re wasting your time. Just go get a copy of Mine because chances are you’ll love it too.<br /><br />EDIT: Forgot to add this, but Mine is NOT in Remy's POV. All in Brooke's.....<br /><br />~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br /><br />I’m going to be ranting so apologies ahead of time. <br /><br /><b>
  <u>If you like books with exaggerated intensity, this is the one for you.</u>
</b><br /><br />This writing is...<i>interesting.</i> *cocks head* What I mean is it’s intriguing enough for me to read through the book, yet it brought forth so much anger and annoyance. I think the overly descriptive, almost poetically fluffy paragraphs were meant to induce lust, to force the reader to <i>feel</i> the tangibility of Brooke and Remy’s love, to sugarcoat the non-existent plot, to <i>think</i> that when all of these words are put together, somehow it’s supposed to turn up the intensity dial. Needless to say, <b>it.did.not.</b> <br /><br />How many times do I need to read about the hollering crowd in the fight scenes, each person just <i>dying</i> to get a piece of Remy? Was this part of the plan to increase the hype and adrenaline levels? It got old and exaggerated.<br /><br /><b>
  <i> “REMY!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!”<br /><br />“RIP-TIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIDE!”<br /><br />“Riptide, you put the sex in SEXY!”<br /><br />“RIPTIDE! RIPTIDE!<br /><br />“Remy, I want you to fucking impregnate me!”</i>
</b> &lt;--- oh PLEASE honey...*rolls eyes*<br /><br /><b>
  <i> “The one, the only, RRRRRRRRRRiiiiiippppppppppptiiiiiiiiiiiiiiiiide!”</i>
</b><br />^^I may have missed a couple of "i"s in there.<br /><br />I don’t know about you, but after the third or fourth drawn-out hollering, I wanted to cover both of my ears and hurl myself off a cliff. I ended up skimming through these fighting scenes because half of the time it would be all these people screaming and the other half was when the referee would shout “knockout.” Whooohooo yeah, yeah Remy, you won your fights. <br /><br />As for the flowery descriptions of, well, <i>everything</i>, I really could care less about. From Remy’s lickable abs to his muscled arms and chest to Brooke’s forever-soaked panties to listening to Iris a million times to- You get the point. I truly think that these descriptions comprised 90% of the book, the other 10% being the meager story plot. Somewhere along the way, the author lost me. Drowned me with all of these unnecessary paragraphs and paragraphs about abs or eyes or dimples or legs... *skips pages*<br /><br /><b>
  <u>If you like whiny, insecure heroines, then this is the book for you</u>
</b><br /><br />There’s no way to sugarcoat this: I don’t know what the heck Remy sees in Brooke. You know that in the previous book Brooke leaves a heartbreaking letter for Remy when she left him. As a result, Brooke discovers some not-so-pleasant info about what happens to Remy after she left him and now struggles with more jealousy and insecurity. My reaction? One, Brooke you LEFT his ass so stop moaning, groaning, and crying your eyeballs flat. Two, why is this even brought up here? I personally saw it as extra drama and besides, wasn't it all resolved in the first book? I guess the author found it necessary to add it here. The most aggravating part?! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[You find out that all this drama was for NOTHING. =_=  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />And when Brooke is <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[pregnant <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, that opens up another can of boring and predictable. Next.<br /><br /><b>
  <u>If you like having secondary and tertiary characters come and go without adding much to the story plot, then this is the book for you.</u>
</b><br /><br />This book is a repeat of Real. Why, why, why, why, WHY did everything have to go back to Nora? Were there no other plausible storylines to go with?! Didn’t like her involved in Real. Didn’t like her involved in Mine. I have a feeling she’ll be in Remy too. <br /><br />Pete and Riley. Oh you two….what to say about them? These two are loyal to Remy like no other, and would do and say <i>anything</i> to prevent his mood episodes from happening. Note the emphasis on <i>anything</i> since their actions brought forth completely preventable drama. <br /><br />The parents. I mean, really, how old is Brooke again?! Twelve? Someone give me a drink...And Remy's parents? A-holes, the lot of them. This was probably the one scene where I felt something for Remy. <br /><br /><b>
  <u> If you like redundancy and “it’s so stupid it’s laughable” scenes, then this book is <i>definitely</i> for you.</u>
</b><br /><br />If you’ve read Real, you probably know all about people giving instructions to Brooke. Don’t do this. Sit here. Don’t make eye contact. Don’t give him a reason to come over here. Eat this. Blah blah blah. This book was the exact same, except the scenes got even more outrageously funny. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>“All right, if Remington knows he just flipped you off and you just flipped him...”</i>
</b><br /><br />What? What? WHAT? What’s going to happen huh Pete? A girl can’t express her opinions and give ‘em the bird? As the crowd says, BOOOOOOOOOO!<br /><br />Something I NEVER understood since Real was, why the heck does Remy need Brooke to look him in the eye and smile in order for him to fight well? Oh gosh, I can just hear it. The little angels flying around my head saying: “Because it’s loooooooooooove.” *rolls eyeballs*<br /><br />The cynical me just laughs at this. Because literally every fight, Remy needs to see Brooke in order to do well, and if she doesn’t smile back/frowns/looks away/doesn’t look at him, he falters. DUDE. WTF happened to your balls? If you believe Remy letting himself getting hit equates to his massive, ginormous, out-of-the-world love for Brooke, then…well, you believe it. *shrugs*<br /><br />After thinking about this book for a day, I bumped it down to 2.5 stars. 3 stars would signify that it was somewhat enjoyable, and had some new stuff in the plot. Mine didn’t have that effect on me. I started and stopped this book three times, and each time left me more annoyed than the last. Eventually I just had to power through the last 50 pages, which was even more jumbled up. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Remy is fighting Scorpion, no restrictions, Brooke looks for Nora, the fighting place is a mess, and then Brooke is going through labor. Seriously, did everything have to be crammed into one scene? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I also thought the loose knots with Nora and Scorpion were tied up too fast and without much explanation. <br /><br />In this book’s defense, I did read Mine right after finishing my most favorite series in the world so I was still stuck in a semi-book hangover. But for the hype this book was getting, along with the rave reviews, Mine was a huge disappointment. <br /><br /><br /><i>ARC provided by publisher via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="5765401080147107914" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer757684286" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12442309335510849192"><b>WARNING: Spoilers Ahoy</b><br/><br/>Meet the real hero of this book:<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384547519ra/6899815.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>No, this is not Remington Tate. This is Adam Wilson, credited by Katy Evans as her editor. In her Acknowledgments, she neglects to mention that Adam is currently in residence at the Simon & Schuster Psychiatric Ward For Editorial Personnel. Adam is currently listed as suffering from "exhaustion" and "dehydration." (And we all know what <i>that</i> means.) He's also on the shortlist for a liver transplant because his alcoholic intake rocketed into th</span>
  <span id="freeText12442309335510849192" style="display:none"><b>WARNING: Spoilers Ahoy</b><br><br>Meet the real hero of this book:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384547519ra/6899815.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>No, this is not Remington Tate. This is Adam Wilson, credited by Katy Evans as her editor. In her Acknowledgments, she neglects to mention that Adam is currently in residence at the Simon &amp; Schuster Psychiatric Ward For Editorial Personnel. Adam is currently listed as suffering from "exhaustion" and "dehydration." (And we all know what <i>that</i> means.) He's also on the shortlist for a liver transplant because his alcoholic intake rocketed into the stratosphere once he commenced his editorial duties on this masterpiece.*<br><br>Sometimes heroes fail, but that doesn't make them any less heroic. Adam had a monumental task before him, so it comes as no surprise that he couldn't succeed. He's been tested and tried in the past. His author slate includes Christina Lauren (of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16102004.Beautiful_Bastard__Beautiful_Bastard___1_" title="Beautiful Bastard (Beautiful Bastard, #1) by Christina Lauren" rel="nofollow noopener">Beautiful Bastard</a> fame) and the cannot-kill-the-corpse-of-VC-Andrews. Prior to joining Simon &amp; Schuster, he was an editor at MIRA &amp; Harlequin TEEN.<br><br>Literary shitburgers &amp; Adam Wilson are not strangers. He's looked into the abyss many a time.<br><br>But I feel a quiver of sympathy for the man. Imagine the bolt of terror that must have shot through Adam's vitals when he opened the mailing envelope sealed with pink heart stickers, withdrew the manuscript of <i>Mine</i> and began to read....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384563210ra/6903405.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For anyone who has read or followed a friend's reading progress of <i>Real</i>, you know what to expect from the pen of Katy Evans: idiotic grammar, garbled syntax, mangled similes, a few words repeated so often they start to look funny, and a hero who likes to play with his semen and manually shove it up his lady love's hooha as a demonstration of Possessive Twu Wuv. Even cavemen think that's going a little far.<br><br>Really, the saga of Brooke &amp; Remy has been something speshul ever since it landed on the self-pub circuit. But since it got picked up by Simon &amp; Shuster, I was curious to see what good some "professional editorial oversight" might produce. Turns out, not a lot.<br><br>I'm not knocking Adam Wilson. Either he was born with no soul, or he's found the right pills &amp; booze combo to forget he has one.** Or Katy Evans is so secure in her mediocrity that she is an earnest force of nature that slays whatever is in her path. Now that I've read her second offering, I'm going with that conclusion.<br><br>Believe it or not, the first...eh...twenty percent was noticeably different from <i>Real.</i> Yeah, it was still crap with Brooke obsessing about Remy's physical perfection and her crotchular feelz, but it didn't eat away at my will to live <i>too</i> much. Sure, it started out with copious amounts of humping and drooling over Remy's quads and deltoids and mentioning his spiky hair and blue eyes a few times on every page. Which was followed quickly by Brooke's insane leap into Drama Llamaland in The Case of Remy and the Whores. (How dare he sleep with other women after I left him?!?) Peppered with the New. Adult. Punctuation. That fucking. Sucks.<br><br>But....<i>but</i>....there was Barely. Any. Clenching.<br><br><b>INORITE?!??</b><br><br>I was actually thinking, "Huh, maybe this'll rate TWO stars."<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384547604ra/6899836.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I should have known it wouldn't last. Should have known that Katy was chomping at the bit to get her cray-cray groove going and just FUCK ALL RESTRAINT. And at 22% she made her editor run screaming for the hills when Brooke accepts a package from Remy's nemesis <b>Benny</b> and the scorpions leap out and sting her all over.<br><br>And the downhill roll commenced. Really. It wasn't exactly like flipping a switch from super-edited high quality to utter crap, but after the scorpions reared their sassy little stingers, this book started going off the rails.<br><br>By the end, I seriously couldn't believe what I was reading. It was unleashed Katy Evans Id, even <b>worse</b> than <i>Real</i>, and that's a phrase I hoped I would never have to type.<br><br>The medical research malfeasance from Book 1? I'll see your Bipolar fetishization and raise you:<br>* <i>"They put me on pills, but it worsened pretty bad. The only thing that got me out of it was my family and Melanie, exercise and sun."</i> (Brooke's sob story that she suffered from depression tooooooo....for all of two months.)<br><br>* <i>"I'd also read about a 'kangaroo method' where the nurses set the baby against the mother's bare skin to strengthen and mature all of his systems."</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384557783ra/6902425.gif" width="267" height="150" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>* The horse tranquilizer that Remy's handlers jab into his neck whenever he goes manic (because that's healthier than lithium) is discarded in favor of even more ridiculous extreme crap. This time, electroshock treatments that can be gotten whenever he feels too speedy. Rules and regs don't apply when you're an MMA fighter who wants to love up your woman with your eyes blue instead of black.<br><br>* Brooke loses all track of her period because her "arm thingy birth control" did such a good job of <i>eradicating it entirely,</i> even when it's six months' expired. Therefore, in true dipshit romance heroine fashion, she gets knocked up.<br><br>* Remy's holy seed fetus is a bit fractious and doesn't want to stay put. (It's probably pretty crowded in there, what with all the old semen plugs clogging up space.) After Brooke starts to miscarry and gush blood at one of the fights, she's given a cream to rub on herself and they can't have sex. However, this doesn't stop them from engaging is really lame Skype sex with Brooke's womb in a perpetual state of contraction. I haven't had the dubious pleasure of pregnancy or miscarriage so I'm no expert, but as with everything else scientific that Katy Evans has utilized, the drama factor is far more important than fact. Rubbing a cream on yourself doesn't sound like it'll stop <i>anything</i> beyond a rash.<br><br><b>And the motherfucking prize of rage:</b><br>* <i>"There’s so much evidence vaccines could be the cause of autism."</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384557783ra/6902424.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Onward to the plot (such as it was):<br>Remember the subplot of Brooke's sister Nora being the drugged-out ho of The Scorpion? Well, you get <b>the same thing again</b>. With minor tweakage, but just as with Book 1, the only "plot" that motivates events is provided by Nora running off with The Scorpion. This time, it's over a sex tape of Nora's which will <i>embarrass</i> Remy and Brooke, and so she caves to Benny's blackmail. That raw and ripped Underground MMA fight circuit....they're such <i>prudes.</i> I'm sure fans who scream at ringside about getting pounded by Remy's cock would clutch their pearls over a sex tape. *hella skeptical* When did sex tapes become shocking career killers again?<br><br>There's more. So much more.<br><br>Even MMA fights have weight classes. Remy is up against opponents who range from sounding like his build to guys who <i>bend the floor</i> when they walk. But of course we're seeing everything described through Brooke's eyes, and she insists that molten lava is flowing through her veins, her insides are twisting like pretzels, tears <i>"are literally exploding from my eyes"</i>, and can discern that her crotch is <i>jealous</i> of her mouth when giving Remy a BJ, so yeah. Worst reliable witness EVER.<br> <br>God, it's all so fucking dumb.<br><br>For the record, all this dumb shit occurs <i>after</i> the box of scorpions. I still think the editor had high-tailed it out of there and lied bourbon-soaked lies that he had read - and approved - of the rest.***<br><br><b>No one in their right mind would think this was good.</b> And there is nothing and nobody in the story who could redeem it. Certainly not Remy - who is a personality cipher, a growling muscled lump of spiky black hair, overdescribed eyes, and licks like a lion. (Oh, I have the data.) And definitely not Brooke, who has traded in her clenching for whiny insecure jealousy. EPIC amounts of whiny, possessive, insecure, irrational jealousy. These idiots are two jealous asshole peas in a pod. So why has Brooke been the one to get so much hate in some of the reviews with Remy getting a pass?<br><br>There is such a psychology Master Thesis about this genre begging to be written.<br><br><b>In Closing:</b><br>With the kind permission of the author of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/593448585" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <i>The Ode to the New Alpha</i>
</a>, I bring you a new verse: <i>Ode to the New Alpha's Female</i>.<br><br>Speshul snowflakes with token flaws,<br>Only their besties aren't botoxed bags of slut.<br>Their parents are dead or simply don't understaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaand<br>And "Tiny_Violin.mp3" is on Repeat.<br>Baste them in baby batter, or shove it in there.<br>It'll make them clench and drool.<br>Growly "Mine"s make them gush. And gush.<br>Watch your step! That's not water on the floor!<br>______________<br><i>(* Not a word of this is true. Unlike the author of this book, I will own up to my bullshit.)<br>(** Again, I'm making it allllll up.)<br>(*** Bourbon-soaked lies have their place. This isn't one of them.)</i><br><br><b>THE DATA (as accurate as possible):</b><br>Spiky (wrt hair) = 11<br>fucks her ear = 1 or 2<br>Brooke sees Remy fucking her in his head = 4<br>fucks her name = 1<br>fucks her mouth (with his tongue) = 2<br>eye-fucking = 2<br>slick = 15<br>hyperaware = 5<br>splat/splattered = 11<br>Brooke's clenching (womb/tummy/heart/pussy) = 10 <i>(Adam Wilson, I salute you!)</i><br><i>Remy's</i> clenching (muscles/jaw/fists) = 11 (!!!!)<br>lion = 20<br>lick = SEVENTY FUCKING SIX<br>scent = 28<br>Remy's eyes (blue/black/dark/flash/glimmer/glinting/dancing/sparkling/"territorial, fuck-my-mate look" blah blah blah, etc.) = ONE HUNDRED FUCKING-SHOOT-ME SIXTY-NINE<br>Mine (grunting alpha/insecure jealous doormat context) = 68 (Because titling it <i>Mine</i> simply wasn't enough)<br>Mine (regardless of context) = numbers don't go that high</span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/588315454?book_show_action=true">Apr 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer588315454" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10191598197485728836"><b>4.5 I love REMY stars!</b> <br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/cf2a1b76-e05f-4765-9d7d-03e9686eb383_zps8e1e8a66.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383658964i/6626384.jpg' alt='Mine photo cf2a1b76-e05f-4765-9d7d-03e9686eb383_zps8e1e8a66.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I HATE reviewing books like this! Hate it! You want to know why... because if I reviewed the book how I wanted to, there would be so many spoilers no one could read it. So... I’m just going to have to be a little vague about some things and tell you what I loved- with no spoilers of course :D<br/><br/><i>Real</i> was a hit or miss book for a lot of people. For me, it was a hit. And there is one particular reason for that. His name is Remington Tate. <br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/6d8c3758-7973-420e-a092-a03f550f8d84_zps683c04c5.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383658964i/6626385.jpg' alt='Mine photo 6d8c3758-7973-420e-a092-a03f550f8d84_zps683c04c5.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>
  <blockquote>Nobody taught him how to love</blockquote></b></span>
  <span id="freeText10191598197485728836" style="display:none"><b>4.5 I love REMY stars!</b> <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/cf2a1b76-e05f-4765-9d7d-03e9686eb383_zps8e1e8a66.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383658964i/6626384.jpg" alt="Mine photo cf2a1b76-e05f-4765-9d7d-03e9686eb383_zps8e1e8a66.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I HATE reviewing books like this! Hate it! You want to know why... because if I reviewed the book how I wanted to, there would be so many spoilers no one could read it. So... I’m just going to have to be a little vague about some things and tell you what I loved- with no spoilers of course :D<br><br><i>Real</i> was a hit or miss book for a lot of people. For me, it was a hit. And there is one particular reason for that. His name is Remington Tate. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/6d8c3758-7973-420e-a092-a03f550f8d84_zps683c04c5.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383658964i/6626385.jpg" alt="Mine photo 6d8c3758-7973-420e-a092-a03f550f8d84_zps683c04c5.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <blockquote>Nobody taught him how to love. He does it instinctively.</blockquote>
</b> There is something about Remington Tate. Remy fights hard but loves harder. He is protective, possessive, alpha male to the extreme. There is nothing I don’t love about Remy. He is sweet, considerate, sexy as hell, and yes, he is damaged. Everything with his family has messed him up. He goes into ‘black’ periods, but he tries his best to control them. Brooke wants to help him, but sometimes just being there for him is enough.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/a2fa07cb-80ff-45d9-a192-194b200c3b67_zps63b0b38f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383658964i/6626386.jpg" alt="Mine photo a2fa07cb-80ff-45d9-a192-194b200c3b67_zps63b0b38f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Brooke still isn’t my favorite heroine, but I have to say that she annoyed me much less in this book than in Real. I’m happy to report that she grew up some. She wasn’t perfect, but I think she made better decisions overall regarding Remy and how she reacted to him. I really do love Remy and Brooke together. The raw, real, possessive and powerful love they have. Their love never falters. They want each other. They need each other. <br><i>
  <blockquote>“You,” he says, his voice terse and commanding as he drags his wet thumb across my lips, “are going to love me until I die. I’m going to make you love me even if it hurts, and when it hurts, I’m going to make it better, Brooke. You’re going to fucking love me if it kills us.”</blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/a6213f40-94b1-4bbb-b116-43d65c05fc3a_zps82119ef4.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383658964i/6626387.jpg" alt="Mine photo a6213f40-94b1-4bbb-b116-43d65c05fc3a_zps82119ef4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <blockquote>“I promise. I promise, you have my heart, and you have me. You will always have me.”</blockquote>
</i><br>Things I loved- I love the way Remy and Brooke communicate with music, I always have. I think that is one of the most beautiful things about their story. I love how deeply and passionately they feel for one another. While reading, you can feel the passion between the two. And the sex. The sex was HOT. Mine had it’s predictable parts in the story line. For that reason, I didn’t love this one quite as much as I did Real. For fans of Real, I would recommend picking it up! If you haven't read Real, what are you waiting for, you NEED to meet Remy! And for those that didn’t love Real, you probably won’t love Mine either. That being said, Mine was a great read for me! <br><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/789fc877-9726-47b6-80b6-676cb0930d90_zpseb57eaa5.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383658964i/6626388.jpg" alt="Mine photo 789fc877-9726-47b6-80b6-676cb0930d90_zpseb57eaa5.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>When everything’s meant to be broken I just want you to know who I am.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><i>**ARC provided by publisher for blog tour via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review**</i><br></span>

    <a title="Geri Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11757728-geri-reads"><img alt="Geri Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487874758p2/11757728.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/588188688?book_show_action=true">Apr 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Geri Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Geri Reads" href="/user/show/11757728-geri-reads">Geri Reads</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer588188688" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1590712469746199547"><b>DNF at 43%</b><br/><br/>Okay, fine! I shouldn't have read this!<br/><br/><a href='http://imgur.com/6j82lpd' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383835602ra/6680367.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I thought I should give this one a try. For one, this series was picked up by a publisher and maybe, just maybe, it would make somewhat of a difference. With a solid editor behind her, who knows where the story of Remy and Brooke will take us. But I was wrong.<br/><br/><a href='http://imgur.com/GN9rjnZ' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380434498ra/876985.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>For one, Brooke just wouldn't shut up about how cut Remy's muscles were or how blue his eyes were. Or his scruffy jaw, his dimples and his eight pack, plus the scenting and licking...</span>
  <span id="freeText1590712469746199547" style="display:none"><b>DNF at 43%</b><br><br>Okay, fine! I shouldn't have read this!<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/6j82lpd" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383835602ra/6680367.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I thought I should give this one a try. For one, this series was picked up by a publisher and maybe, just maybe, it would make somewhat of a difference. With a solid editor behind her, who knows where the story of Remy and Brooke will take us. But I was wrong.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/GN9rjnZ" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380434498ra/876985.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>For one, Brooke just wouldn't shut up about how cut Remy's muscles were or how blue his eyes were. Or his scruffy jaw, his dimples and his eight pack, plus the scenting and licking...Gah!! <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/UsOFI3n" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381328024ra/4711519.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Even Remy's fights gets repetitive. Do I really need to read the announcer yelling, "RIPTIIIIIDEEEEEE," every single fight he has? Do I really need to hear the groupies shout inane statements like, "Remy, I want to have your babies," every fight? Or the crowd yelling or chanting, "Riptide?"<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/KLkOltG" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380791426ra/3122901.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The repetitiveness killed this story for me. That and the fact that I felt this story is totally unnecessary.I don't need another book in Brooke's POV. The girl is annoying as hell. She's whiny and ungrateful and she doesn't deserve Remy one iota. And honestly, the fact that Remy is in love with this girl makes Remy less hot in my eyes. He'll always be known as the guy who's in love with a stupid girl that everybody hates. That makes him less hot to me.<br><br>So Katy Evans....You win! I.Give.Up. <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/XOHNgWw" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383832969ra/6679773.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Edit:</b>And until now, no one can explain how in the heck Remy can afford a posse of coaches, nutritionist, trainers, stay in first-class suites and have a private jet while fighting in an underground league. The math just doesn't add up. <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="1590712469746199547" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_762353232" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/762353232" />
    <a title="Katy Evans" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16938241-katy-evans"><img alt="Katy Evans" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1467129779p2/16938241.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/762353232?book_show_action=true">Nov 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katy Evans" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katy Evans" href="/user/show/16938241-katy-evans">Katy Evans</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span> (Review from the author)


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer762353232" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16844183205381789238"><br/>I am so excited that Brooke and Remy are back in their readers hands! I have a very soft spot for MINE. I think some books are very easy to write, and some are very hard. MINE was easy to write, but hard to let go of, because it's the near-end of Brooke and Remy's story for me, and it was a ride which I just loved taking.<br/><br/><br/>Where did Brooke and Remington go after Real finished? I just had to find out. <br/><br/>My goal writing MINE was not recreating REAL, for REAL is already written. My goal was going deepe</span>
  <span id="freeText16844183205381789238" style="display:none"><br>I am so excited that Brooke and Remy are back in their readers hands! I have a very soft spot for MINE. I think some books are very easy to write, and some are very hard. MINE was easy to write, but hard to let go of, because it's the near-end of Brooke and Remy's story for me, and it was a ride which I just loved taking.<br><br><br>Where did Brooke and Remington go after Real finished? I just had to find out. <br><br>My goal writing MINE was not recreating REAL, for REAL is already written. My goal was going deeper, pulling out their imperfections and their demons and have them prove to me that even then, good or bad, they were in it for each other. In MINE I wanted Brooke to prove to me, through all her challenges, that she was capable of standing by Remy, even when she had her own little demons to battle. I wanted to watch her grow, mature, for her man. For HIM.<br><br>And Remy, well, we all know what he'd do for her. He has his demons, and I wanted to know more about them, and I wanted to see him cope being with or without her. I love the fact that they are both so flawed, so passionate about the other, he's a lion and she's his little firecracker. I love how Brooke's feistiness brings out the alpha in him, how I could feel their love on every page, animal, raw, and just like Mr. Tate ordered. <br><br>Brooke and Remy have a total of three stories; REAL, MINE and REMY, and to me, each of them represent a stage in a relationship. Real is the lust, the falling in love, the mystery and excitement. Mine is when it gets real. When you see your other half is not perfect, but you love them anyway. Mine is the challenges, the growth, the devotion and the proof. And finally, Remy. From his POV, Remy is a little bit of present, of Real, and of Mine, and it rounds up their story in a way that left me extremely happy.<br><br>I am beyond grateful for the book love we've received! For you taking the time to read, and write or leave your notes and reviews,it is all very appreciated. <br><br>Whether Mine is for you or not, I give them to you as I saw them, lived them, and loved them, and I hope that you can open your heart like I did and enjoy the ride which made me smile, laugh, happy, sad, broken, and whole.<br><br>All my love.<br><br>Katy Evans<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/authorkatyevans/media/thinkofmelikecrazy_zpsbddf63e6.jpeg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384193604i/6809775._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo thinkofmelikecrazy_zpsbddf63e6.jpeg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="16844183205381789238" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer602678914" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1027521495913068650"><br/>Interview with Katy Evans, visit <a>HERE</a> <br/><br/>Book Signing Photos with Katy Evans, visit <a href='http://jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com/2013/11/mine-real-2-by-katy-evans-book-signing.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>HERE</a><br/><br/><a href='http://imgur.com/7Z8j3oL' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383659449i/6626519._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>4.5 Oh My Remy Stars</b> <br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I’m the realest fucking thing you’re ever going to have</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> <br/>If you are looking for an alpha, over-loaded, gripping, pull-your-hair-out, tension, over-maxed read, well Mine is for you.<br/> <br/>Let’s just get all the ass kissing out of the way first… Katy Evan, damn. Katy writes in a way it seems like poetry. Most of my book is highlighted, in fact, I had to reframe from highlighting becau</span>
  <span id="freeText1027521495913068650" style="display:none"><br>Interview with Katy Evans, visit <a>HERE</a> <br><br>Book Signing Photos with Katy Evans, visit <a href="http://jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com/2013/11/mine-real-2-by-katy-evans-book-signing.html" rel="nofollow noopener">HERE</a><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/7Z8j3oL" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383659449i/6626519._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>4.5 Oh My Remy Stars</b> <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I’m the realest fucking thing you’re ever going to have</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> <br>If you are looking for an alpha, over-loaded, gripping, pull-your-hair-out, tension, over-maxed read, well Mine is for you.<br> <br>Let’s just get all the ass kissing out of the way first… Katy Evan, damn. Katy writes in a way it seems like poetry. Most of my book is highlighted, in fact, I had to reframe from highlighting because most of the pages were yellow! <br> <br>Oh how I love Remy. I loved Real and I loved Remy. He’s the kind of guy you just want to rip your clothes off for and let him have his way with you. When I first picked up Mine, I kind of thought it was going to be more Brooke’s story (hence the cover), but it really isn’t. Mine is still the continued story of Remy and Brooke.<br> <br><a href="http://imgur.com/zMbZ0iP" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383659449i/6626520._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br><b>So… what can we expect?</b> <br><br>Lots of steam… sex... including, petting, licking, biting, nipping, sucking, smelling… you got that?<br> <br>Crazy damaged, alpha, tatted, made-of-steel boxer<br> <br>Somewhat highly emotional and crazy Heroine (but totally justified).<br> <br>Your heart will be beating A MILLION MILES a minute from start to finish.<br> <br><a href="http://imgur.com/njqxMDT" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383659449ra/6626521.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br><a href="http://imgur.com/A5XpN3T" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382926469ra/6283791.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br>Mine was a difficult read for me. There are few things that make it hard for me to read books and Mine touched on of those issues. Also, I know I’m crazy, I’m not a fan of angst and although Mine wasn’t “angsty” there were a lot of moments where I just had no idea what was going to happen and it was over whelming… in a good and bad way. Good because it makes the writing great, bad, b/c I could have had a heart attack!<br> <br><a href="http://imgur.com/M4ujgGJ" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383010273i/6333311.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>You’re everything I never knew I wanted. <br>I adore you with every breath I take – in every ounce of me, I adore you</b>
</blockquote> <br>I am always cautious in reading sequels, because I love the characters so much, I really don’t want them to struggle anymore, BUT Katy did well. Although there were some slow moments, overall MINE was a fast face read (if that makes sense). I really enjoyed Remy and Brooke’s dynamics.<br> <br>I love damaged Remy, he’s so real, raw and gritty. I also loved how Katy described him as a lion and a tree, these sort of descriptive words, really put Katy, as an author, to a whole new level (I know, I said I wouldn’t ass kiss anymore, but I can’t help it, she’s good!).<br> <br>Brooke is a mess, but in a justified good way. You understand her struggles and you sympathized, she’s still trying to get over pass and present issues. I wouldn’t say most of the tension is between Remy and Brooke, there are a few external forces that come to play. Which I loved! I love it when it’s the couple against the world kind of read.<br> <br><a href="http://imgur.com/BayGNtM" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383659449i/6626522._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>You are going to love me until I die. I’m going to make you love me even if it hurts, and when it hurts, I’m going to make it better, Brooke <br>Ripped, raw and so real. He’s all mine – or at least, that’s all I want in the world. For him to be mine.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> <br>My final point to cross is that, if you are a Real fan, you will love Mine, it’s different, but still raw, real and sexy as ever. <br> <br>**Quotes were taken prior to publication and is subject to change**<br> <br><i>An ARC was provided in exchange for an honest review</i><br> <br><b>Series Order</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17617277.Real__Real___1_" title="Real (Real, #1) by Katy Evans" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1363442697s/17617277.jpg" alt="Real (Real, #1) by Katy Evans" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> | <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/585854939" rel="nofollow noopener">REVIEW</a> | <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00CRAMM02/ref=as_li_qf_sp_asin_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=211189&amp;creative=373489&amp;creativeASIN=B00CRAMM02&amp;link_code=as3&amp;tag=jacqsread-20" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17792606.Mine__Real___2_" title="Mine (Real, #2) by Katy Evans" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1377178049s/17792606.jpg" alt="Mine (Real, #2) by Katy Evans" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> | <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00D0MZXCA/ref=as_li_qf_sp_asin_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=211189&amp;creative=373489&amp;creativeASIN=B00D0MZXCA&amp;link_code=as3&amp;tag=jacqsread-20" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer588388744" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17878517710156802048"> <b>5 Fighting Stars!!</b><br/>	<br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383732515i/6647665.jpg' width='450' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Brooke and Remy are finally together and happy, a new promising season is beginning and things finally start to look good for them.<br/>Despite some remains of anger towards Brooke departure, things are finally solid between them. <br/><br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383732515ra/6647666.gif' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>But then a life-changing event occurs and force them to be apart for some time. And with the distance comes insecurity. Brooke starts to feel insecure about all the groupies, about the fighting and everything that comes with it. <br/>And Remy’s problem are </span>
  <span id="freeText17878517710156802048" style="display:none"> <b>5 Fighting Stars!!</b><br>	<br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383732515i/6647665.jpg" width="450" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Brooke and Remy are finally together and happy, a new promising season is beginning and things finally start to look good for them.<br>Despite some remains of anger towards Brooke departure, things are finally solid between them. <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383732515ra/6647666.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But then a life-changing event occurs and force them to be apart for some time. And with the distance comes insecurity. Brooke starts to feel insecure about all the groupies, about the fighting and everything that comes with it. <br>And Remy’s problem are not helping him dealing with all the distance between them.<br>So now that’s all in the verge of breaking they have to find out if now is the time to fight… or if is time to submit and end the match. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383732515i/6647667.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This was so GOOD. There was a time when Brooke annoyed the hell out of me, but Remy, oh-sweet-and-sexy-Remy, he made it all worth it. <br>It was a little predictable, but the steam was all there and it was also sweet and romantic with no end. <br>If you liked the first one, YOU HAVE to read this. Like… now. </span>
  <a data-text-id="17878517710156802048" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer10031594654407249923"><b>4 Ripped, Raw, and so DAMN Real Stars<br/><br/><i>“Mind. Body. Soul. All of you for me. All of you mine.”</i></b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380403627i/785234.jpg' width='400' height='333' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>Here he is, ladies and gentlemen. Here. He. Is! <br/>You all know who I’m talking about?” <br/>“RIP-TIIIIIIIDE!” <br/>Who?  <br/>“RIP-TIIIIIIDE!” <br/>One more time, ’cause I can’t hear you! <br/>“RIPTIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIDE!”<br/><br/>“That’s right, ladies and gentlemen!"<br/>The one, the only, Remingtoooon Tate, your RIPTIIIIIIIIIDE!!”</b>

But life isn</span>
  <span id="freeText10031594654407249923" style="display:none"><b>4 Ripped, Raw, and so DAMN Real Stars<br><br><i>“Mind. Body. Soul. All of you for me. All of you mine.”</i></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380403627i/785234.jpg" width="400" height="333" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>Here he is, ladies and gentlemen. Here. He. Is! <br>You all know who I’m talking about?” <br>“RIP-TIIIIIIIDE!” <br>Who?  <br>“RIP-TIIIIIIDE!” <br>One more time, ’cause I can’t hear you! <br>“RIPTIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIDE!”<br><br>“That’s right, ladies and gentlemen!"<br>The one, the only, Remingtoooon Tate, your RIPTIIIIIIIIIDE!!”</b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414118i/816124._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When love is the answer to all your questions you think you have it all. But life isn't that easy. It keeps throwing curveballs your way. Fight and do it dirty. Kick and punch. And in the end is not the stronger that will emerge winner. It's the braver and the one who managed to stood up that eighth time that he stumbled and no one expected him to make it. Like <b>Remy</b> the gifted fighter who has suffered all his life and every day is a struggle. And like <b>Brooke</b> who lost all her dreams to realise that the ones she didn't dare make where just waiting for her.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405518i/790041.jpg" width="400" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Normal is overrated and possesive is the NEW sexy!<br><br><pre>Holy freaking hell Remy got to me again!</pre><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380391734ra/754278.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380419459ra/831593.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380414864ra/818398.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Delicious, sexy, heartbreakingly emotional and passionate this book is like an altar to worship the alpha male. From scenting and licking to swoon-worthy gestures, romantic music and panty-melting sex scenes. From Brooke's point of view we witness the magnificence of an athlete that his body is his temple and has found the other half of his tortured soul. The light in his existence to fade the "black". And make it acceptable. <br><br>This book lacked the intensity of the first and Brooke's insecurities got old really fast. But deep inside my inner-fangirl got loose and even now she is shouting that she won't let me down-vote her Remy at all. She also managed to get ahold of my well-hidden cavewoman and together they are conspiring against me. Rumor has it that they are looking into lions for some strange reason... Maybe 'cause of that licking?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383859985i/6689261._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>A beautiful love story with enough sexiness to put you on fire! Don't miss these books...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/576746.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Continue reading for my pre-review rant...</i><br><blockquote>
  <b>

More Remy, my fellow fangirls!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417639i/826300._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="610" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380409196ra/801106.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer1716648116124365515"><b>
  <u>My Thoughts:</u>
</b><br/><br/>❥ This story picks up two months after <i>Real</i> ends and we get to find out what's been going on with Brooke and Remy. <br/><br/>❥ IMO, it was a lot of the same with a little bit of the different. I felt that Remy had matured a lot and had more of a handle on Brooke and his condition. Brooke, on the other hand, seemed less able to deal with things especially since she caused most of the problems. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383888380i/6697541.jpg' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>❥ Remember all the sexual tension in the first book? Well, that's gone and instead we get scene af</span>
  <span id="freeText1716648116124365515" style="display:none"><b>
  <u>My Thoughts:</u>
</b><br><br>❥ This story picks up two months after <i>Real</i> ends and we get to find out what's been going on with Brooke and Remy. <br><br>❥ IMO, it was a lot of the same with a little bit of the different. I felt that Remy had matured a lot and had more of a handle on Brooke and his condition. Brooke, on the other hand, seemed less able to deal with things especially since she caused most of the problems. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383888380i/6697541.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>❥ Remember all the sexual tension in the first book? Well, that's gone and instead we get scene after scene of peaking, throbbing, licking, scenting....it all just seems to run together after a while. I was actually glad when the sex was over so we could get to something else! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379798937i/647717.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>❥ Don't get me wrong, we get that Remy is hot but I'm not sure we need to hear about his 8 pack, his dimples, his spiked hair and all his muscles over and over again!<br><br>❥ I did love the times when they just cuddled and especially when they played songs for each other. And I loved the whole play on the King and Queen! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1441000648ra/16050951.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>❥ The drama with Scorpion continues and there's some interesting little twists going on. <br><br>❥ Something also happens between Brooke and Remy...not that you couldn't see it coming and I'm still not sure how I feel about it. It also seems too cliché. But one thing's for sure, I won't ever believe that Remy would leave her...nope, not buying it. <br><br>❥ Racer...LOL! Not even remotely what I would have thought. Now Iris...yes, that was wonderful. I was really hoping for something poignant. <br><br>❥ All in all, I did enjoy the book. There is just something about it that pulls me in. I love the connection between the two of them especially the songs. But the repetition was killing me! I cannot wait for the next book and Remy's POV. <br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/655824.gif" width="400" height="070" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>Favorite quotes:</u>
</b><br><br>♫ “Forgive me. I forgave you, little firecracker. I forgave you before you even asked me to forgive you for leaving me. I wasn’t me when you left, baby, whatever pieces of me remained . . . that wasn’t me.”<br><br>♫ “You’re everything I never knew I wanted.”<br></span>

<div id="review_1227613616" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1227613616" />
    <a title="Snow" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31719636-snow"><img alt="Snow" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1465808156p2/31719636.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1227613616?book_show_action=true">Mar 14, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31719636-snow?shelf=best-ever">best-ever</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31719636-snow?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31719636-snow?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31719636-snow?shelf=5-star-read">5-star-read</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1227613616" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer903195808657952124"><br/><b>6 "LOVE OF A LIFETIME" stars<br/><br/>overwhelmed again...and speechless at the moment...<br/><br/>RE-READ IT January 8, 2017.</b><br/><br/>Ah, I'm back to do the hardest thing I had to do lately - give my humble thoughts on this piece of gem, right here...<br/><br/>Gosh, what can i say! I thought that book 1 was good, no, but fan-f*cking-tastic! cause it was! but this, this was as equaly stunning, beautiful and overpowering!<br/><br/>It's rare to stumble across the characters that grip you by the balls (well, that would be the case if I actually h</span>
  <span id="freeText903195808657952124" style="display:none"><br><b>6 "LOVE OF A LIFETIME" stars<br><br>overwhelmed again...and speechless at the moment...<br><br>RE-READ IT January 8, 2017.</b><br><br>Ah, I'm back to do the hardest thing I had to do lately - give my humble thoughts on this piece of gem, right here...<br><br>Gosh, what can i say! I thought that book 1 was good, no, but fan-f*cking-tastic! cause it was! but this, this was as equaly stunning, beautiful and overpowering!<br><br>It's rare to stumble across the characters that grip you by the balls (well, that would be the case if I actually had balls LOL) but let's just stick to the saying for the dramatic tone!<br><br>I'm fascinated by the easy flow of words, yes i could actually predict what would/could happen next but it didn't matter cause I was magicaly enchanted by him - <b>Remington "Remy" Tate aka Riptide</b><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>My fighter. He fights everything, even himself, but I love that he’s never fought loving me.<br><br>My playful boy, my protective man, my jealous boyfriend, my cocky fighter. My misunderstood little boy.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444072910i/16448457.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>the man was <b>imperfectly perfect - his outside shell was perfect to protect the imperfect and flawed inner being...and he's fighting it - he's trying God damned hard to control it, to make it as acceptable as possible for her - the woman that ripped his heart, glued it back nad healed it back again, his persistance to overcome the "bad" or "wrong" for the sake of "good" and "right" is admirable and praise worthy</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444072910i/16448458._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“You don’t have to understand me—just love the hell out of me. Can you do that? Can you?” His thumb drags with sensual roughness across my lower lip. “Do you?”<br><br>“You,” he says, his voice terse and commanding as he drags his wet thumb across my lips, “are going to love me until I die. I’m going to make you love me even if it hurts, and when it hurts, I’m going to make it better, Brooke.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444072910i/16448459.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“I want you. I want you to touch me, to put your lips on mine—like before. I want you to love me. Stop fucking punishing me, Brooke. I love you.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>It's a bit difficult to sum up all the things that are roaming through my head and I really don't wanna re-tell the story, cause that's not the point now, is it?<br><br>the story itself is not something you haven't read before and there's nothing new to add - they are two people who are dealing with their relationship discarding the worse out of the bad and accepting the reality of it... <br><br>BUT <b>the essence</b> of it is the amount of emotions that I felt while reading it! I literally could feel every single emotion they felt and I was going through the situations along with them, I was driven by their choices and I could just be there in their heads...thinking, re-thinking, agreeing, disagreeing, making a statement...aknowledging it all<br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>He’s a man who falls and gets up again and again. He pushes, plows, plunders, goes on.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>and one of the important segments of their growth as individuals and as a couple was through the lyrics of their favorite songs and that is something i can relate to...cause I do that, like a lot!!!! LOL<br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Didn’t you hear the songs!? They were all for you, Brooke. Didn’t you know I thought of you? Missed the hell out of you? If I haven’t showed you I love you, then tell me in what ways I’m fucking this up!”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426877473i/14113694.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>music is an entity that is always in my background, around me, with me, beside me, in me...I can't live without it, I can't even "be" without it! <b>and to feel them connecting through music, through lyrics when your own words aren't loud enough, when the vibration of notes and lyrics emphasize the significance of touch...<br><br>even when they were apart...music was the connection that made them survive</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426877473ra/14113695.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>Love, lust, need course through me as I come and thrash beneath him.</b>
</i><br><br>touch - what held my heart like a cramp and would not let go until I finished, was the sense of love as they felt it for each other, but it was more then love itself - the intensity of it was higher than the feeling itself, the passion was palpable and flammable and scorching hot BUT what I felt through it, was - pure need, the belonging - it was home.<br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Baby, the way you need me can only barely cover half of the way I need you.”<br><br>“God, how I need you.” He props his forehead on mine and drags in a coarse breath. “How I go crazy thinking of you. The whole flight on my way here I listened to the song you’ve played to tell me you love me.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>This was f*cking beautifuly written love story!<br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“I love, adore, cherish, need, and want you like I never thought possible to love and adore and cherish and need and want another human being or anything in this world,”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>this was a love story to die for...<br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Like you said, I’ll love you if it kills us,” I whisper as I stroke his face. “We all die. I’d rather die loving the hell out of you.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>it takes just one soul, that one breath, the power that consumes you, another being to call MINE<br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>Black and blue, every inch of you, magnificent you, is mine. And I’m going to treasure and cherish you, always.<br><br>“Yes, Remy, it’s really all about you.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>I feel like a little girl again, the big dreamer, with all those longing sighs spent imagining if that kind of love really exists...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426877473i/14113696.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>I'd like to think/believe that it does.</b><br><br>p.s. October, 5th 2015. i just decided that Micah Truitt will be my Remy permanently! Signed, sealed, delivered!<br></span>

<div id="review_588261694" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/588261694" />
    <a title="Jen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6049062-jen"><img alt="Jen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460575899p2/6049062.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/588261694?book_show_action=true">Apr 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen" href="/user/show/6049062-jen">Jen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=kindle-own">kindle-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=new-adult-romance">new-adult-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=november-reads">november-reads</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer588261694" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14812717767246134535">Oh dear..where to begin with this one? I wanted to love it, I truly did..and I was so looking forward to this second book. Unfortunatly, this book just really did rub me the wrong way. There were some good parts to it, one of them being my fierce and studly Remy! ( I mean, it is hard NOT to fall in lust for him! )The whole book though, just felt like the author took the popular phrases from the first book; and over used them in this one. It almost made me feel uncomfortable while reading it, bec</span>
  <span id="freeText14812717767246134535" style="display:none">Oh dear..where to begin with this one? I wanted to love it, I truly did..and I was so looking forward to this second book. Unfortunatly, this book just really did rub me the wrong way. There were some good parts to it, one of them being my fierce and studly Remy! ( I mean, it is hard NOT to fall in lust for him! )The whole book though, just felt like the author took the popular phrases from the first book; and over used them in this one. It almost made me feel uncomfortable while reading it, because these phrases were repeated so much. I am sad to say that for a majority of the book, I actually began to skim. Even with my skimming, I didn't miss alot, because there was just so much of the same things being said and done. There is only so much of the couple licking and smelling each other that I can take before it becomes extremely annoying. I began to cringe each time it was mentioned that Remy licked behind Brookes ear, or every time the couple smelled one another in the crook of their necks. It just felt like a lot of "filler" instead of a story full of substance.<br /><br />I feel strongly that the first book, Real; should have been a stand alone book with a kick ass epilogue. I truly loved that book, it was intense and electric when Remy and Brooke first laid eyes on one another. The sex was so wonderfully primal, and just plain HAWT!! For some reason, it just didn't work this second time around. I think because it got old very fast. I would have loved some fresh material to get excited over.<br /><br />There were parts of the story that I did enjoy. Mostly, when anything new happened. In those cases, I became involved and eager. I feel that I gave this installment a fair chance. I really wanted to love it. "Real" will still always be a book that I will have fond memories of; but I don't even think that I could re-read it now because everything just became "Blah" and I now need to move on from the experience.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="14812717767246134535" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

I don't mind a woman being vulnerable or dickmatized or even emotional... but there needs to be a balance. It definitely received all four of those stars for the wonderfulness that is Rem</span>

Every single page is like a secret...like something beautiful that can't wait to settle in my heart. I loved every moment even the ones that made my heart hurt.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383791061i/6667983.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383791061i/6667984.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383791061i/6667985.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b><br>5 million Sizzling Hearts &amp; Stars !!!!!!</b>
</i><br><br><br>Everybody that knows me knows that REAL was my all time favorite steamy romance of 2013. I told everyone about this blue eyed licking lion. I made my one and only book trailer for this.<br><br><br><a href="http://snack.to/pdksv5s8" rel="nofollow noopener">~Real~ Katy Evans</a><br><br>(I kinda stalked Katy Evans, and this gracious lady is so freaking humble. I'll always adore her) <br><br>I had never even written a real review until REAL (Pun intended)<br>I was in a book funk for so long and didn't ever in a million years think that Mine could live up to what REAL did to my heart. <br><br>PEOPLE I WAS SO WRONG. Mine blew me away! I loved it more than REAL and that is a big deal to me. <br><br>Remy and Brooke just did something to my heart. I think it all began with reading about Remy's childhood and that he was "discarded" and pushed away. My heart broke for this beautiful human being. <br><br>Brooke steps in and immediately starts showing Remy this amazing love that he so deserved.<br><br><blockquote>
  <br>
  <b>"I want him more than any one of these screaming women wants</b>
  <br>
  <br>
  <b>him. I want every fragmented part of him. I want his body. His mind.</b>
  <br>
  <br>
  <b>His heart. His beautiful soul."</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Brooke loved Remy with everything in her and I felt so happy for him to finally have somebody that would fight and stand by his side no matter what. I was so mad at Brooke in REAL at the end when she left him in that hospital bed and I knew that her actions would come back to haunt her. When she encountered what those actions may have done to their relationship while apart, my heart broke with her. <br><br><b>"I’m</b><br><br><b>not perfect. I’ve never been taught to do this. I never dreamed of</b><br><br><b>love, a partner "</b><br><br>You'll have to read Mine to understand exactly the roller coaster this <br>took me on. I felt so strongly the utter despair that Brooke felt and <br>how I knew in heart ..that something wasn't right.  I won't give anything away but just know that Remy is the most loyal true and honest character I have ever encountered. He never ever lets you down. <br>When Remy shows his love ..he not only shows it, he completely immerses Brooke in his love.<br><br>Their passion burns the pages and you can't help but be swept away. Remy is so possessive and loving and just perfect. I want to reach in my<br> Kindle and pull him out. His scenting, licking and petting is just over<br> the top amazing.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383791061i/6667986.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I can only imagine what thoughts will be portrayed in his POV coming up in Remy.<br><br>He loves from the bottom of his beautifully damaged soul and Brooke was what he wanted , who he loved and he made sure she knew it.  <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383791061i/6667987.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So many things happened in Mine that just made me fall in love with this couple more and more. <br><br>Brooke grew to someone I felt respect for by the end and I felt her love helped heal Remy in more ways then one. She helped give him more than just a woman's love, she was his biggest supporter and his best friend. But most of all she gave him a family. Something he never really felt apart of.<br><br>Brooke saw not what was broken in Remy, she saw what was whole..his beautiful heart ...his amazing strength and his steadfast loyalty. She knew he deserved every ounce of her adoration , every single second of her devotion and she was determined to let him know how much he was loved.<b><br>"God, I love him, and I never want him to forget it!"</b><br><br>Katy has a way with words, she has a way with reaching and grabbing you by the freaking heart. I loved every moment. Her song choices again were spot on. But the one song that really spoke to me, that really portrayed the love between Brooke and Remy is below.<br><i>
  <b><br><br> Kelly Clarkson Darkside<br><br> everybody's got a dark side<br><br> do you love me?<br><br> can you love mine?<br><br> nobody's a picture perfect<br><br> but we're worth it<br><br> you know that we're worth it<br><br> will you love me?<br><br> even with my dark side?<br><br> don't run away<br><br> don't run away<br><br> just tell me that you will stay<br><br> promise me you will stay<br><br> don't run away<br><br> don't run away<br><br> just promise me you will stay<br><br> promise me you will stay<br><br> will you love me?<br></b>
</i><br>Brooke loved him, she promised she'd stay and even though she ran once...she made up for it a billion times making sure her knew he was her <b>
  <i>REAL</i>
</b> always. I am so excited to start Remy this week and Katy is still in my top favorite people ever. I am so eager to also find out what she has in store for us in Ripped and Raw coming up in the next year. Katy, I'm in utter awe and just one more time, Thank you for your brilliance, imagination and creative soul! <br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383791061i/6667988.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383791061i/6667989.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
