        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer588243554" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11676762844601804958">Ummm, so yeah. When I finished Real, I could NOT wait to read more of Remy and Brooke. And don't get me wrong I really really liked this book, but there were a few things that irritated me too. <br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384724655i/6940943._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>BEWARE FOR SPOILERS</b><br/><br/>This is the second book in the Real series. It picks up 2 months after Remy and Brooke have gotten back together and everything is smooth sailing. They are either training, fighting in the Underground, or screwing. Happy Times, until Scorpion decides to come back around and then...... </span>
  <span id="freeText11676762844601804958" style="display:none">Ummm, so yeah. When I finished Real, I could NOT wait to read more of Remy and Brooke. And don't get me wrong I really really liked this book, but there were a few things that irritated me too. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384724655i/6940943._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>BEWARE FOR SPOILERS</b><br><br>This is the second book in the Real series. It picks up 2 months after Remy and Brooke have gotten back together and everything is smooth sailing. They are either training, fighting in the Underground, or screwing. Happy Times, until Scorpion decides to come back around and then...... a life changing oops happens. :) <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384724655ra/6940944.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved Remy in this book. He had so many battles to fight and was so sweet and so freaking hot. SWOON!!!! However, Brooke really began to irritate me. Her inner thoughts became almost too much and repetitive. I mean I get some of the insecurities, really I do, but Remy did everything to prove himself to her and still she went on and on. And then the licking and smelling thing. OMG!!! In Real, I actually thought it was cute, totally cute. And I didn't mind it in this book at all, except that it seemed like every other sentence it was being mentioned. And even though I still loved it, it got to the point all I could imagine was them running around with spit baths and smelling like each others spit. LOL, I know it wasn't meant to be that way but it was mentioned so much that that got stuck in my head. <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384724655ra/6940945.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384724655i/6940946._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My only other complaint <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ is Brooke and Remy with their baby. I may have read too much into this, but to me, it almost seemed like an afterthought on more than one occasion. I can't really explain it. Other than, sometimes they seemed more into each other than really caring about the baby. Like they only liked her pregnant because there was a piece of Remy in Brooke for the world to see that was staking a claim to each other and that made them feel more connected. Then the brief time we saw them with the baby after it was born, they were both impatient with it needing to eat because they wanted to get it on. I've been there, done that, with a new baby, I think it was just the way it was written that it made me feel like that. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Like I said, I may have blown that way out of proportion, it was just the way it came across to me. I was more into the first 40% of the book than the next 40% and then the last 20% got me back into it again. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384724655i/6940947._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Other than that, it was a good read. I didn't like it as much as the first book, but still liked it a lot. I will say I was relieved to see that the 4th and 5th book isn't about Brooke and Remy. I was wondering where the story would be able to go after this. I am very very very excited to read Remy's book though. Like, can't wait!!! <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384724655i/6940948.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>April 15, 2013<br>This is me begging for Remy soon, hahaha!!!<br><br><a href="http://gifsoup.com/view/429758/usher-begging.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417329ra/825257.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://gifsoup.com" title="GIFSoup" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">GIFSoup</a><br><br>I need more Remington Tate, NOW!!! So Excited for More. :)</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

    <a title="Michelle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle"><img alt="Michelle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505605297p2/13126896.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle">Michelle</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer589969895" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12000844784542032018"><b>I am completely torn about this story. I loved every second of Remington ‘Riptide’ Tate and if I could solely base my rating on him it would be 5 stars. But Brooke drove me nuts and made me want to scream at my Kindle. I think I will settle someplace between a 3.5 & 4 stars.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383722705i/6644248._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Mine begins just where Real left off. Remy has his Brooke back and they are off for the next season in The Underground. But they still have the challenges of his mood shifts and Scorpion isn’t yet history. But both Brooke an</span>
  <span id="freeText12000844784542032018" style="display:none"><b>I am completely torn about this story. I loved every second of Remington ‘Riptide’ Tate and if I could solely base my rating on him it would be 5 stars. But Brooke drove me nuts and made me want to scream at my Kindle. I think I will settle someplace between a 3.5 &amp; 4 stars.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383722705i/6644248._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Mine begins just where Real left off. Remy has his Brooke back and they are off for the next season in The Underground. But they still have the challenges of his mood shifts and Scorpion isn’t yet history. But both Brooke and Remy have to come to terms with what her leaving did to him. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>”Remington has been abandoned his whole life. Parents. Teachers. Friends. Even me. Nobody has ever stuck with him long enough to show him he’s worth it. What he did, just to get me to touch him and give him some love, makes me burn to drown him with my love until he never, ever has to ask for it.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>This is their story of the fight to win. Both in and out of the ring. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383722705i/6644249.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><i> I tried really hard to see where Brooke was coming from, but I failed. After reading Real there was zero doubt in my mind how much Remy loved her. How important she was to him. But Brooke’s insecurities and constant flood of tears worked my nerves. For a while it felt like it was either her lusting after him or crying over him. <br><br>There is zero doubt in the ability of Katy Evans to create a sex scene that has the readers lusting for more, but where we had such sexual tension in Real, I felt like it was a bit overwhelming in parts. I honestly think that may have to do solely with my frustrations with Brooke though. I just could not seem to get past her issues.<br><br>Remy was where this book had me. He was primal, possessive and gentle. There was such a difference in his character in the shifts from blue to black that did not exist before. Because now he had his real, he had Brooke. <br> <br>We also saw a heartbreaking side to his life and just how much he fights to survive. These moments broke my heart. <br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<blockquote><i><b>”When?” I cry.<br>“When you were gone and we had to keep him from slitting his fucking wrists because of you!”</b></i></blockquote>
<br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>I think we all fell in love with Remy from the start and there is nothing that would ever keep me from reading more of him or really anything Katy Evans publishes. <br><br>Overall my own expectations might have let me down or I am just getting to that point of frustration with annoying heroines that just can’t seem to have any self-worth, trust in the person they love or any rationality in their thinking.<br><br>I am looking forward to Remy, getting to see his point of view in various scenes and hopefully seeing Brooke mature and realize that now that Remy has his real, he isn’t going to let anything take it away.</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383722705i/6644250._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417578i/826108.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="12000844784542032018" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_588380456" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/588380456" />
    <a title="Ang (Sizzling Pages)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13629682-ang-sizzling-pages"><img alt="Ang (Sizzling Pages)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1541857150p2/13629682.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/588380456?book_show_action=true">Apr 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ang (Sizzling Pages)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ang (Sizzling Pages)" href="/user/show/13629682-ang-sizzling-pages">Ang (Sizzling Pages)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer588380456" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5454758539978948778">For more reviews please visit and join<br/><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://angelas-sizzling-pages.blogspo'>http://angelas-sizzling-pages.blogspo</a>...<br/><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.sizzlingpages.com'>http://www.sizzlingpages.com</a><br/><br/><b>3.5 stars</b><br/>ARC provided by the author in exchange for an honest review<br/><br/><br/>This review was difficult for me. I am going against the grain on this one, and I know that my viewpoint will not be a popular one. I did not love “Mine”. I liked it, but I struggled through this read. I really, really tried to get into it, but certain things bothered me and they could not be over looked. Regardless, I would</span>
  <span id="freeText5454758539978948778" style="display:none">For more reviews please visit and join<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://angelas-sizzling-pages.blogspo">http://angelas-sizzling-pages.blogspo</a>...<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.sizzlingpages.com">http://www.sizzlingpages.com</a><br /><br /><b>3.5 stars</b><br />ARC provided by the author in exchange for an honest review<br /><br /><br />This review was difficult for me. I am going against the grain on this one, and I know that my viewpoint will not be a popular one. I did not love “Mine”. I liked it, but I struggled through this read. I really, really tried to get into it, but certain things bothered me and they could not be over looked. Regardless, I would like to thank the author for sharing her story and Remy, who is an amazing alpha-male.<br /><br />Remy’s character saved the book for me. He was strong, both physically as well as emotionally. He maintained control of his circumstances and the highly sensitive, erratic train wreck that was Brooke, in spite of his ailments. I adored the way he handled her, loved her, worshipped her, and soothed her. He is a powerful and erotically sensual man. He’s the example of the perfect alpha-male and his flaws made his character more appealing. All that is Remy, the lion, kept my interest in this story.<br /><br />Brooke, on the other hand, was far from appealing to me. What makes a character fascinating is watching their persona grow and evolve as the story progresses. It just did not happen with Brooke. She was immature, selfish and irrational at times. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[(Brooke really turned me off during the time she was on bed rest. She should have been focused on her medical condition rather than how hot she gets for Remy or if he is being faithful to her – really Brooke, that’s all you care about? There are more important things in life. Your responsibility was to take care of your “condition” and not get off on Remy).  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Towards the very end of the story, her character began to show a slight growth, which was a bit too late in the game.<br /><br />I felt an opportunity was missed in this tale. Most of the story was dedicated to Brooke’s amorous feelings for Remy. How she loved him, how he turned her on, how horny he made her feel, how protective and “proprietary “ Remy is of her. The description of her feelings and affections seemed to go on and on, page after page. Leaving me to wonder when will the story pick up? Where’s the angst? Why not more conflict with Scorpion (Remy’s nemesis)? I wanted fewer declarations of love and more “meat and potatoes” in this story. Again, by the time it started to pull together, it was towards the finale.<br /><br />Lastly, to end on a positive note, the love scenes were sizzling hot, proving that Remy is “the man”. Brooke’s love letter was sweet and, as always, I adored the way these two lovebirds communicated their feelings through song. I do look forward to reading Remy’s POV in the next installment of this series. His character is fascinating and cannot wait to see the world through his eyes.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5454758539978948778" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer595169582" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13502501212664906341"> <b>5 REEEMMMMYYYYYYYY, scent, lick, suck and taste, stars*****</b><br/><br/><i>How on earth do I review a book I just love so much without giving away the plot? I'm going to try my best but for me even though the story is a delight and had me sweating, salivating and feeling like I'm a dog on heat it's really to me about the characters and especially one special beautiful Lion which is.....</i> <br/><br/><b>REMY...</b> <br/><a href='http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/real%20and%20mine%20by%20katy%20evens/null_zps155accc2.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383856179i/6687359._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo null_zps155accc2.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><a href='http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/real%20and%20mine%20by%20katy%20evens/remy2_zps4d76dc9c.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383856179i/6687360._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo remy2_zps4d76dc9c.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>He just blew me away he really is the epitome of Alpha! He is raw, strong, sexy, he is built like a Lion, fig</span>
  <span id="freeText13502501212664906341" style="display:none"> <b>5 REEEMMMMYYYYYYYY, scent, lick, suck and taste, stars*****</b><br><br><i>How on earth do I review a book I just love so much without giving away the plot? I'm going to try my best but for me even though the story is a delight and had me sweating, salivating and feeling like I'm a dog on heat it's really to me about the characters and especially one special beautiful Lion which is.....</i> <br><br><b>REMY...</b> <br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/real%20and%20mine%20by%20katy%20evens/null_zps155accc2.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383856179i/6687359._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo null_zps155accc2.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/real%20and%20mine%20by%20katy%20evens/remy2_zps4d76dc9c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383856179i/6687360._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo remy2_zps4d76dc9c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>He just blew me away he really is the epitome of Alpha! He is raw, strong, sexy, he is built like a Lion, fights like a king but he has a HUGE heart. He takes cares of the people he loves but mainly Brooke she is his, he nurtures her and protects her. How would it feel to be loved like that, its what us girls crave, right? <br>When I was reading this to me this was a beautiful soul deep love story I had butterflies in my tummy like we were just meeting for the first time, he had me in bits every word on those pages come out and seep through. There's just doesn't seem to be the right words to depict the Image and love that is Remy.. <br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/real%20and%20mine%20by%20katy%20evens/mine1_zps4e65e175.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383856179i/6687361._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo mine1_zps4e65e175.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I read a lot of Alpha males who love and protect there women but really Remy screams Alpha to the core. Then there's his heart, and what he's dealing with day to day. There's his vulnerability and I just want to jump in and grab a hold of him myself. His doubt, does he deserve to be loved? Should he be medicated? Is he dealing with his mental health the best way he can? <br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/real%20and%20mine%20by%20katy%20evens/null_zps01cf4303.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383856179i/6687362._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo null_zps01cf4303.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>With Remy theres those BLACK times:<br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/real%20and%20mine%20by%20katy%20evens/null_zpsd26fd17e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383856179i/6687363._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo null_zpsd26fd17e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And how he deals with them:<br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/real%20and%20mine%20by%20katy%20evens/remy1_zpsc9f8301d.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383856179i/6687364.jpg" alt=" photo remy1_zpsc9f8301d.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And then theres the Blue:<br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/real%20and%20mine%20by%20katy%20evens/bluerose_zps75f198dd.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383856179i/6687365._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo bluerose_zps75f198dd.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>BROOKE</b><br> <a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/real%20and%20mine%20by%20katy%20evens/brooke_zpsc6deaef8.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383856180i/6687366._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo brooke_zpsc6deaef8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>I believe there are some mixed reviews for this being people are frustrated/infuriated by Brookes insecurities and jealousies yes I agree in some aspects but mainly I didn't find her to be that bad, I enjoyed the tears and she does have a lot on her plate, how would you deal? <br><br><b>And then there's the licking, tasting and scenting!!!</b><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/real%20and%20mine%20by%20katy%20evens/makelovegif_zps3414fa79.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383856180ra/6687367.gif" alt=" photo makelovegif_zps3414fa79.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/kissing/kissingbitegif_zps047d428d.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382653910ra/6097246.gif" alt=" photo kissingbitegif_zps047d428d.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>THE MUSIC</b><br>I have to say I loved the music every new song I found myself looking through ITunes and listening while I was reading, it did make my reading there story a much more enjoyable experience. There music was as much about this book as the story. <br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/real%20and%20mine%20by%20katy%20evens/listeningtomusic_zps1f977b80.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383856180i/6687368.jpg" alt=" photo listeningtomusic_zps1f977b80.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So to conclude you get that I enjoyed there journey but really I found Katy Evans really did depict how you deal with a mental health problem, how they love deep and how they cherish the people around them, and especially for giving us REMY he will forever be in my heart. <br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/hitheregif_zpsd5a96048.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/580012.gif" alt=" photo hitheregif_zpsd5a96048.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

    <a title=" ~*~Princess Nhya~*~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3055882-princess-nhya"><img alt=" ~*~Princess Nhya~*~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595187086p2/3055882.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/589283487?book_show_action=true">Apr 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title=" ~*~Princess Nhya~*~" class="user" itemprop="url" name=" ~*~Princess Nhya~*~" href="/user/show/3055882-princess-nhya"> ~*~Princess Nhya~*~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer589283487" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6776251785275456242"><b>Solid 1.5 Stars</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1135.photobucket.com/user/Enhya77/media/justfyi_supernatural.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381230810ra/4566977.gif' alt=' photo justfyi_supernatural.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/>Now let's be clear... The only reason why I stayed here was because of <b>Remy..</b> And my love & hope that came from book 1(Real) But unfortunately, like a marriage, it takes more than one person to keep the boat afloat. <b>Brooke</b> completely sunk this ship for me. I'm not happy about it. As a matter of fact, I'm beyond disappointed with her. But that's not the only thing I'm unhappy about.<br/><br/>Case & point... <b>Contrived Plot</b> throughout this entire book.<br/><br/><b>1.</b> From chapter 2 & beyond, all <b>Brooke</b></span>
  <span id="freeText6776251785275456242" style="display:none"><b>Solid 1.5 Stars</b><br><br><a href="http://s1135.photobucket.com/user/Enhya77/media/justfyi_supernatural.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381230810ra/4566977.gif" alt=" photo justfyi_supernatural.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Now let's be clear... The only reason why I stayed here was because of <b>Remy..</b> And my love &amp; hope that came from book 1(Real) But unfortunately, like a marriage, it takes more than one person to keep the boat afloat. <b>Brooke</b> completely sunk this ship for me. I'm not happy about it. As a matter of fact, I'm beyond disappointed with her. But that's not the only thing I'm unhappy about.<br><br>Case &amp; point... <b>Contrived Plot</b> throughout this entire book.<br><br><b>1.</b> From chapter 2 &amp; beyond, all <b>Brooke</b> did was cry, complain, &amp; show just how utterly insecure she is as far as herself, her relationship with <b>Remy</b> &amp; their circumstances. She's whining about stuff that she knew she was already gonna have to deal with when she decided to be with <b>Remy</b> It's not like she wasn't aware. She seen these things for herself before she even got involved with him. It just comes with the territory as far as his profession goes. Yet here she is acting all hurt &amp; jealous &amp; cooking up all kinds of ridiculous thoughts in her head &amp; being a brat about it towards him in the process. At the worst possible times mind you. Yet it's so blatantly clear to the reader &amp; the other characters in the book, where <b>Remy's</b> loyalties lie. Why doesn't <b>Brooke</b> see this? <br><a href="http://s1135.photobucket.com/user/Enhya77/media/cs.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397855ra/768116.gif" alt=" photo cs.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>2.</b> I was not at all happy about the MAJOR turn this story took concerning these two. There are many reasons why this should not have happened, IMO. <b>Ms Evans</b> should never have taken it there. And the fact that it was also used as a catalyst to explain Brooke's irrational, irritating behavior, made me loathe this plot development even more. The fact that this book was once again told in Brooke's POV does not help matters cos all she does is obsess. About Remy's body, about her unreasonable insecurities &amp; back &amp; forth. It got beyond ridiculous. So much so I was left reacting this way...<br><a href="http://s1135.photobucket.com/user/Enhya77/media/tumblr_lxwup7Wxa11qi53v3_zpsa55d72c0.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384180183ra/6804553.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_lxwup7Wxa11qi53v3_zpsa55d72c0.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>We've never needed a Male POV more than we do in this book. I needed <b>Remy's</b> thoughts here. I needed to see exactly what it is he saw &amp; loved about Brooke through his eyes. I simply just needed to be in his space without a 3rd party narrative. I needed to hear his thoughts in his own words. Especially during his dark times. Because Brooke, just wasn't doing it justice. I think it would have made for a more reasonably dramatic &amp; poignant tale that Ms. Evans was trying to convey, but just missed the mark greatly by using Brooke's voice. Or should I say using a voice that has nothing deep to say.<br><br> Also, there is a big difference between having a <i>Great love in your life</i> &amp; that love <i>BEING YOUR LIFE</i> In Brooke's case this was NOT a good thing. 90% of her thoughts, feelings &amp; emotions were directly dependent upon Remy &amp; <i>his</i> world. I think if there had been more balance with this &amp; we got it in healthy doses, it wouldn't have been an issue with me. But cos we never got it in that vein, this bothered me a lot. <br><br><b>3.</b> The mess with Brooke's sister <b>Nora</b> was a complete dud/let down. Really? <i>That</i> was the big mystery behind what she was doing? Are you kidding me? I never liked her sister anyway. But, still... And <b>Scorpion,</b> considering what he did in book 1 &amp; what he did in the beginning of this story, I really feel like his "Semi-Demise" was a bit anti-climactic. Though I really don't feel like this is the total end for him. Considering that little brief exchange between he &amp; Remy before it was "lights out" but still in this book, his "ending" was lacking.<br><br><b>As you can see</b> I hated this book. Honestly, if you're an author looking to extend a series on the same characters, then come up with an actual plot &amp; not a gross extension of more of the same. <b>Brooke's</b> constant insecurity/whining was not only unoriginal, it totally ruined this book. We needed <b>Remy's</b> POV here. Badly. A real plot (not a lame revisit of a subplot concerning her sister) but a real &amp; new plot, with growth in the characters being the name of the game. <br><br>I loved book 1. And after reading book 2, I think this should have never been made into a series. There were so many avenues that <b>Ms Evans</b> could have taken with this book concerning <b>Remy &amp; Brooke.</b> But she chose the easiest, most common &amp; irritating route. And the fact that the <b>3rd book "Remy"</b> is just going to be a recap of what we already know from book 1, just solidifies my point that this should have never been made into a series. <br><br>So back to my original statement, <b>Remy</b> is what made this book for me. Though you don't get enough of him, what you do get is beyond intense, sexy, sweet &amp; endearing. It's just unfortunate that his other half wasn't able to make it complete.<br><br>So no, I can't in good faith say that I would recommend this read. You're taking a risk if you read it. It could go either way for you.<br><br><br><br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="6776251785275456242" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('AUh5sdCQydJSWHp2sYzjdMz7tWLwSZGoSjj2Ahpm+uw7bhBja84AuvVzzhdGeemrGqRSqj7EH88RRrCz1yUIdg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('rFu1GuzIYA2fmW2NA8PHlIzokkc1+5Dgdib6oLc1wWSWfdzIV5apZTiy2ez0Ns1LWrd1j/t2HoctWLwRenYz/g==')})
  }
